		// GET SIZE OF AN SLOT AND ADD DATA HEIGHT PROPERTY TO HIS FATHER
		googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
			if ( event.slot ){
				var divSlot = $("#"+event.slot.getSlotElementId());
				if ( $(divSlot).data("format") == "double" ){
					try {
						var alto = parseInt(event.size[1]);
						if ( alto < 600 ) {
							var idComplement = $(divSlot).parent().find('.adblock[data-format="complement"]').attr("id");
							console.log("SLOT_ID: " + event.slot.getSlotElementId());
							console.log("REFRESCANDO SLOT_ID: " + idComplement);
							console.log(gptAdSlots[idComplement]);
							googletag.pubads().refresh([gptAdSlots[idComplement]]);
						}
					}catch(e){}
				}
			}
		});
		// KNOW HOW AN AD IS VIEWABLE
		googletag.pubads().addEventListener('impressionViewable', function(event) {

			if (event.slot === gptAdSlots['ad-Roba-Portada']) {
				console.log("viewable");
			}

		});

    if (data.index === 0) {

    }

         <span class="content_wrapper">
          <h2 itemprop="headline">
           <a href="/noticia/yes/2021/03/20/terrazas-reservan-lujo/0003_202103SY20P22991.htm" itemprop="url mainEntityOfPage">
            En estas cinco terrazas gallegas sí puedes reservar
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
           Adiós a las colas. Ya no tienes excusa para salir a tomar algo. Aquí no tendrás que esperar a sentarte. Es llegar y besar el santo. Eso sí, si llamas primero o reservas por la web. Disfruta del buen tiempo con este paseo por las terrazas más recogidas y con muy buenas vistas
          </p>

           <h2 itemprop="headline">
            <a href="/noticia/coruna/2021/03/21/obstaculos-separan-as-xubias-paseo/0003_202103H21C2994.htm" itemprop="url mainEntityOfPage">
             Estos son los obstáculos que hay que salvar para el paseo de As Xubias
            </a>
           </h2>
           <p itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
            Expertos apuestan por soluciones «blandas» para favorecer el ocio y la regeneración de una de las zonas privilegiadas de la ría, en la que hay una vía férrea, un núcleo tradicional y un poblado chabolista
           </p>

          <h2 itemprop="headline">
           <a href="/noticia/yes/2021/03/20/cancer-colon-lado-derecho-puede-tardar-diagnosticar/0003_202103SY20P28991.htm" itemprop="url mainEntityOfPage">
            «El cáncer de colon en el lado derecho se puede tardar más en diagnosticar»
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
           A diferencia de la edad, que no es modificable, hay otros factores de riesgo que sí podemos cambiar para prevenir la aparición de la enfermedad. David Martínez Ares, experto en digestivo, asegura que en unos años la incidencia caerá notablemente
          </p>

  </script>
  <script charset="utf-8" src="/assets/newspaper2017/js/sso.events.js" type="text/javascript">
  </script>
  <script charset="utf-8" src="/assets/newspaper2017/js/sso.min.js" type="text/javascript">
  </script>
  <script src="/assets/newspaper2017/js/jquery.cookie.min.js" type="text/javascript">
  </script>
  <script src="/assets/newspaper2017/js/jquery.jsonp-2.4.0.min.js" type="text/javascript">
  </script>
  <script async="" charset="utf-8" defer="" src="https://cflvdg.avoz.es/assets/themes/lvdg2017/js/min/home.grv-30e8931a27378e420d3b314402a2800f.js" type="text/javascript">
  </script>
  <script>
   var usrtype = 'anonimo';
    var usrlocal = null;
    var usersegments = null;
    var subsname = null;
    var subslife = null;
    var subsperiod = null;
    var subsprice = null;
    var subspromo = null;
    var churnstatus = null;
    var paymentstatus = null;
    var daysremaining = null;
    var daysbonus = null;

    $(document).on('SSO:complete', function(){
        var cookieUsrLgd = $.cookie('ssoUsuario');
        var cookieUsr = $.cookie('_ssoud');
        var cookieSubs = $.cookie('_ssous');
       
        if (cookieUsrLgd != null) {
            usrtype = 'registrado';
            var jsonUsr = jQuery.parseJSON(cookieUsr);

usrlocal = jsonUsr.m;

var usrsegmentsStr = jsonUsr.sg;
usersegmentsArray = Array.from(usrsegmentsStr.split(","));
usersegments = jQuery.map(usersegmentsArray, function( n, i ) {
 return ("SEG"+n);
});

        }
       
        if(cookieSubs != null) {
       
                var jsonCookieSubs = jQuery.parseJSON(cookieSubs);
                switch (jsonCookieSubs.a) {                  
                  case 0:
                    usrtype ='exsuscriptor';
                    break;                  
                  case 1:
                    usrtype ='suscriptor';
                    break;                    
                  default:
                    usrtype ='no definido';
                    break;                
                }
             
                switch (jsonCookieSubs.p) {                  
                  case 'WEB':
                    subsname ='WEBAPP';
                    break;                  
                  case 'ON':
                    subsname ='PDF';
                    break;                  
                  case 'PRO':
                    subsname ='FIN DE SEMANA';
                    break;                  
                  case 'TOTAL':
                    subsname ='7 DIAS';
                    break;                  
                  default:            
                    subsname ='ESPECIAL';          
                    break;                
                }
               
                var subslifemonths = Math.floor(jsonCookieSubs.dc/30);
               
                if (subslifemonths<12) {
                     subslife = 'M'+String(subslifemonths).padStart(2, '0');
                } else {
                     subslife = 'A'+String(Math.floor(subslifemonths/12)).padStart(2, '0');    
                }
           
                switch (jsonCookieSubs.rp) {
                 
                  case '1':
                    subsperiod ='mensual';
                    break;
                 
                  case '2':
                    subsperiod ='trimestral';
                    break;
           
                  case '3':
                    subsperiod ='semestral';
                    break;
           
                  case '4':
                    subsperiod ='anual';
                    break;
           
                  default:            
                    subsperiod =null;          
                    break;
               
                }

                switch (jsonCookieSubs.ip) {                    
                    case undefined:
                        subsprice =null;
                        break;                    
                    default:
                        var subspriceStr = String(jsonCookieSubs.ip);
                        var subspriceStrRep = subspriceStr.replace('.', '-');                        
                        subsprice = 'E-' + subspriceStrRep;
                        break;
                }
       
                switch (jsonCookieSubs.m[0]) {
                    case undefined :
                    subspromo = 'sin promociones';
                    break;
                    default:
                    subspromo = jsonCookieSubs.m[0];
                    break;                
                }
               
                switch (jsonCookieSubs.b) {
                 
                  case 0:
                    churnstatus ='no baja';
                    break;
                 
                  case 1:
                    churnstatus ='baja';
                    break;
               
                }
                               
                if (jsonCookieSubs.a = '1' && jsonCookieSubs.dr != undefined && jsonCookieSubs.dr>0) {    
                   daysremaining = 'DR'+String(jsonCookieSubs.dr).padStart(2, '0');
                   paymentstatus = 'sin incidencias';                              
                } else if (jsonCookieSubs.a = '1' && jsonCookieSubs.dr != undefined  && jsonCookieSubs.dr<0) {
                    daysbonustopositive = jsonCookieSubs.dr*-1;
                    daysbonus = 'DG'+String(daysbonustopositive).padStart(2, '0');
                    paymentstatus = 'error pago';                
                } else {                
                    daysremaining =null;
                    daysbonus =null;
                    paymentstatus =null;
                }
        }
        pintabannerOut(usrtype,usrlocal,usersegments,subsname,subslife,subsperiod,subsprice,subspromo,churnstatus,paymentstatus,daysremaining,daysbonus);
        pintabannerOutMobile(usrtype,usrlocal,usersegments,subsname,subslife,subsperiod,subsprice,subspromo,churnstatus,paymentstatus,daysremaining,daysbonus);
    });
  </script>
  <div id="lvg_mkts_desktop">
   <script>
    function pintabannerOut(usrtype,usrlocal,usersegments,subsname,subslife,subsperiod,subsprice,subspromo,churnstatus,paymentstatus,daysremaining,daysbonus) {            
            googletag.cmd.push(function() {                                
                var mappingOutOfPage = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([1020, 0], [1,1])
				.addSize([768,0],[1,1])
				.addSize([320, 0],[0,0])                  
				.addSize([0, 0],[0,0])
				.build();                
               
                gptAdSlots['lvg_mkts_desktop'] = googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot('/2260323/lvg_mkts_desktop', 'lvg_mkts_desktop')
                .defineSizeMapping(mappingOutOfPage)
                .addService(googletag.pubads());
               
                gptAdSlots['lvg_mkts_desktop'].updateTargetingFromMap({
                                        'usrtype': usrtype,
                    'usrlocal': usrlocal,
                    'subsname': subsname,                    
                    'subslife': subslife,
                    'subsperiod': subsperiod,
                    'subsprice': subsprice,    
                    'subspromo': subspromo,
                    'churnstatus': churnstatus,
                    'paymentstatus': paymentstatus,
                    'daysremaining': daysremaining,  
                    'daysbonus': daysbonus,
                    'usrsegments': usersegments
				});
               
                googletag.display('lvg_mkts_desktop');
                googletag.pubads().refresh([gptAdSlots['lvg_mkts_desktop']]);
               
                var TargetingKeys = gptAdSlots['lvg_mkts_desktop'].getTargetingKeys();
                TargetingKeys.forEach(
                    element => console.log(element + ": " + gptAdSlots['lvg_mkts_desktop'].getTargeting(element))
                );
               
            });
        };
   </script>
  </div>
  <div id="lvg_mks_mobile">
   <script>
    function pintabannerOutMobile(usrtype,usrlocal,usersegments,subsname,subslife,subsperiod,subsprice,subspromo,churnstatus,paymentstatus,daysremaining,daysbonus) {            
            googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                var mappingOutOfPageMobile = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([1020, 0], [0,0])
				.addSize([768,0],[0,0])
				.addSize([320, 0],[1,1])                  
				.addSize([0, 0], [0,0])
				.build();                
               
                gptAdSlots['lvg_mks_mobile'] = googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot('/2260323/lvg_mks_mobile', 'lvg_mks_mobile')
                .defineSizeMapping(mappingOutOfPageMobile)
                .addService(googletag.pubads());
               
                gptAdSlots['lvg_mks_mobile'].updateTargetingFromMap({
                                        'usrtype': usrtype,
                    'usrlocal': usrlocal,
                    'subsname': subsname,                    
                    'subslife': subslife,
                    'subsperiod': subsperiod,    
                    'subsprice': subsprice,    
                    'subspromo': subspromo,
                    'churnstatus': churnstatus,
                    'paymentstatus': paymentstatus,
                    'daysremaining': daysremaining,  
                    'daysbonus': daysbonus,
                    'usrsegments': usersegments
                });
               
                googletag.display('lvg_mks_mobile');
                googletag.pubads().refresh([gptAdSlots['lvg_mks_mobile']]);
               
               
                var TargetingKeys = gptAdSlots['lvg_mks_mobile'].getTargetingKeys();
                TargetingKeys.forEach(
                    element => console.log(element + ": " + gptAdSlots['lvg_mks_mobile'].getTargeting(element))
                );
               
            });            
        };
   </script>
